Mystere's Food Club Results

I would totally recommend you only follow one bettor unless you've got psychic powers. But if that was the case, you should be playing the lotto/betting IRL LOL

So I initially started this page just to keep track of how I was doing with my bets because I was following more than one bettor. September and October's tables are the results from that. I hadn't planned on keeping track of anyone else's bets but have since decided I will, just in case anyone wants to see how each person does daily. I also started making my own bets but hadn't used them during October and I compared how I would have done with them. Based on the results, I'm not too good with bouncing between bettors and would have done better with just my own bets. Yes, I did do better than some bettors, but there were majority that did better than I did.

Sure, some months you could get lucky but I would still recommend just sticking to one.

The people I follow are Garet, Lucy, Sidney (Lefty), JK, Phoenix, Phoenix's Algorithm XXI, Camelia, Marie, Marc, Annie, Jason (Stromm), Sergente (Sergente Hartmann), Nsheng, and Anisa. Nsheng has four sets, Beginner, Standard, Aggressive, and Adventurous.

If you want to take a good look at past comparisons for some of the board chat bettors, take a look at Yehoodi.

Some other bettors out there that also keep track of their daily results or bets are: Crispy, Petra, Mercury, Mina, Jay, Kristina, Riley, Izzy (he usually posts at least two different sets, currently on hiatus) Jada, and Becky.

I keep track of the bet winnings with the help of the data from FCNC to see the bets as they ended up because tables they supply may have had odd changes which could give them, say, a 12:10 instead of 14:10 for example. Although sometimes their is a bit of a glitch or lag and I end up recording an incorrect odd. I will default to the result/wins the bettor has posted themselves rather than what I had seen on FCNC. So if you notice a past odd is wrong, please let me know!

If you are one of the people I am following and you don't want your results shown, please let me know! I'll keep track strictly on paper then. Also, if the results on this page aren't showing up properly if you're viewing them on mobile (sometimes that happens to me) try viewing the results on my other petpage, although it's currently not updated.
